# Derailer Triples Atlas (165 combinations)

Development-oriented descriptions of how *three elevated/high stress traits* can co-occur across life domains. This is not a diagnostic instrument.

**Domains covered per triple:** Career, Business, Friendships, Hobbies, Romantic, Overall lifestyle, Health, Sports.

---

## 1) **VR+WA+IW** — Volatile Reactivity + Worry-Driven Avoidance + Interpersonal Withdrawal

**Signature:** alarm volatility with withdrawal

**Core loop:** uncertainty triggers worst-case thinking and hesitation → communication drops, you go quiet, and you handle things alone → conflict escalates and others experience unpredictability → this reinforces risk-averse and ruminative patterns.

- **Career:** tone spikes, defensiveness to feedback, performance variance across weeks; analysis paralysis; overchecking; delays hard calls and conflict; low updates; quiet in meetings; others lack visibility into work. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Business:** rapid pivots and escalation culture; urgency communicated with heat; slow launches; over-validation; missed windows from hesitation; stakeholders feel cut off; decisions happen privately; low transparency. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Friendships:** intensity cycles; sensitivity to slights; rupture–repair patterns; avoids direct talks; replays interactions; seeks certainty; slower replies; fewer initiations; disappears during busy periods. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Hobbies:** frustration spikes; quits/pauses abruptly or pushes angrily; over-researches; delays starting; fear of doing it wrong; prefers solo versions; avoids groups/communities when stressed. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Romantic:** arguments ignite quickly; push–pull closeness; fast escalation; rumination and reassurance loops; ambiguous cues feel threatening; shutdown during conflict; partner feels locked out; intimacy declines. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Overall lifestyle:** bursts and crashes; routines swing with mood and stress; narrower comfort routines; reduced novelty; mental load stays high; social circle shrinks; solitude becomes default coping. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Health:** sleep disruption/tension; coping volatility (comfort behaviors or overcontrol); insomnia/tension; difficulty relaxing; stress symptoms persist; delays seeking help; under-communicates symptoms; low support use. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Sports:** overreaches after setbacks; heat with coaches/partners; volatile load choices; conservative progression; inconsistent blocks from fear (injury/failure); trains alone; avoids coaching feedback; plateau risk from low input. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.

**Strength edge (when regulated): risk awareness, urgency and energy, independence and focus.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): low transparency / disconnection, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.**

## 2) **VR+WA+CG** — Volatile Reactivity + Worry-Driven Avoidance + Cynical Guardedness

**Signature:** alarm volatility

**Core loop:** uncertainty triggers worst-case thinking and hesitation → tone sharpens, patience drops, and reactions come fast → trust erodes and collaboration becomes defensive and political → this reinforces risk-averse and ruminative patterns.

- **Career:** tone spikes, defensiveness to feedback, performance variance across weeks; analysis paralysis; overchecking; delays hard calls and conflict; defensive interpretations of feedback; accusatory skepticism; paper trails. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Business:** rapid pivots and escalation culture; urgency communicated with heat; slow launches; over-validation; missed windows from hesitation; slow trust-building; hardball negotiations; information hoarding. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Friendships:** intensity cycles; sensitivity to slights; rupture–repair patterns; avoids direct talks; replays interactions; seeks certainty; tests loyalty; assumes slights; keeps score. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Hobbies:** frustration spikes; quits/pauses abruptly or pushes angrily; over-researches; delays starting; fear of doing it wrong; distrusts coaches/groups; assumes agendas; churns communities. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Romantic:** arguments ignite quickly; push–pull closeness; fast escalation; rumination and reassurance loops; ambiguous cues feel threatening; jealousy/monitoring tendencies; conflicts about intent and trust. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Overall lifestyle:** bursts and crashes; routines swing with mood and stress; narrower comfort routines; reduced novelty; mental load stays high; high vigilance; low spontaneity; control behaviors increase. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Health:** sleep disruption/tension; coping volatility (comfort behaviors or overcontrol); insomnia/tension; difficulty relaxing; stress symptoms persist; mistrust of providers; second-guessing advice; nonadherence risk. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Sports:** overreaches after setbacks; heat with coaches/partners; volatile load choices; conservative progression; inconsistent blocks from fear (injury/failure); argues with programming; interprets cues as criticism; coach conflict. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.

**Strength edge (when regulated): risk awareness, due diligence and boundary detection, urgency and energy.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): low trust / defensive interpretation, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.**

## 3) **VR+WA+PP** — Volatile Reactivity + Worry-Driven Avoidance + Passive Pushback

**Signature:** alarm volatility

**Core loop:** uncertainty triggers worst-case thinking and hesitation → you agree outwardly but resist through delay, reinterpretation, or nonfollow-through → conflict escalates and others experience unpredictability → this reinforces risk-averse and ruminative patterns.

- **Career:** tone spikes, defensiveness to feedback, performance variance across weeks; analysis paralysis; overchecking; delays hard calls and conflict; "yes" in meetings, drift afterward; slow-roll; selective compliance. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Business:** rapid pivots and escalation culture; urgency communicated with heat; slow launches; over-validation; missed windows from hesitation; stakeholders experience surprise nonalignment; forecasting and trust suffer. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Friendships:** intensity cycles; sensitivity to slights; rupture–repair patterns; avoids direct talks; replays interactions; seeks certainty; avoids direct conflict; resentment leaks via sarcasm or cancellation. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Hobbies:** frustration spikes; quits/pauses abruptly or pushes angrily; over-researches; delays starting; fear of doing it wrong; ignores guidance; does it "my way" without renegotiating openly. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Romantic:** arguments ignite quickly; push–pull closeness; fast escalation; rumination and reassurance loops; ambiguous cues feel threatening; silent protest and procrastination; indirect retaliation; unspoken resentment. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Overall lifestyle:** bursts and crashes; routines swing with mood and stress; narrower comfort routines; reduced novelty; mental load stays high; resists imposed structure; oppositional routines; chronic friction. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Health:** sleep disruption/tension; coping volatility (comfort behaviors or overcontrol); insomnia/tension; difficulty relaxing; stress symptoms persist; inconsistent adherence if buy-in is low; rebellion breaks and resets. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.
- **Sports:** overreaches after setbacks; heat with coaches/partners; volatile load choices; conservative progression; inconsistent blocks from fear (injury/failure); cherry-picks training; avoids disliked sessions; low transparency about changes. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.

**Strength edge (when regulated): risk awareness, urgency and energy, autonomy and independent judgment.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): hidden nonalignment, slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature.**

## 4) **VR+WA+SI** — Volatile Reactivity + Worry-Driven Avoidance + Self-Importance

**Signature:** alarm volatility

**Core loop:** uncertainty triggers worst-case thinking and hesitation → you dismiss input, centralize decisions, and expect recognition → conflict escalates and others experience unpredictability → this reinforces risk-averse and ruminative patterns.

- **Career:** tone spikes, defensiveness to feedback, performance variance across weeks; analysis paralysis; overchecking; delays hard calls and conflict; dominates airtime; dismisses advice; difficult to coach; credit sensitivity. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Business:** rapid pivots and escalation culture; urgency communicated with heat; slow launches; over-validation; missed windows from hesitation; founder/leader bottleneck; unilateral calls; talent disengagement. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Friendships:** intensity cycles; sensitivity to slights; rupture–repair patterns; avoids direct talks; replays interactions; seeks certainty; one-upmanship; low curiosity; difficulty apologizing. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Hobbies:** frustration spikes; quits/pauses abruptly or pushes angrily; over-researches; delays starting; fear of doing it wrong; resists being a beginner; competitiveness disrupts learning. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Romantic:** arguments ignite quickly; push–pull closeness; fast escalation; rumination and reassurance loops; ambiguous cues feel threatening; power struggles; partner feels unseen or managed. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Overall lifestyle:** bursts and crashes; routines swing with mood and stress; narrower comfort routines; reduced novelty; mental load stays high; status-oriented choices; impatience with constraints; reduced humility. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Health:** sleep disruption/tension; coping volatility (comfort behaviors or overcontrol); insomnia/tension; difficulty relaxing; stress symptoms persist; ignores guidance; exception narratives; delayed preventive care. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Sports:** overreaches after setbacks; heat with coaches/partners; volatile load choices; conservative progression; inconsistent blocks from fear (injury/failure); ego loading; dismisses deloads; injury risk from overconfidence. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.

**Strength edge (when regulated): risk awareness, confidence and decisiveness, urgency and energy.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): slow closure / rumination, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.**

## 5) **VR+WA+BP** — Volatile Reactivity + Worry-Driven Avoidance + Boundary-Pushing

**Signature:** impulsive intensity with higher risk-taking

**Core loop:** uncertainty triggers worst-case thinking and hesitation → you shortcut process, push limits, and act first then manage fallout → conflict escalates and others experience unpredictability → this reinforces risk-averse and ruminative patterns.

- **Career:** tone spikes, defensiveness to feedback, performance variance across weeks; analysis paralysis; overchecking; delays hard calls and conflict; cuts corners; compliance friction; "ask forgiveness" pattern. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rule-bending / high-variance risk, high conflict temperature.
- **Business:** rapid pivots and escalation culture; urgency communicated with heat; slow launches; over-validation; missed windows from hesitation; aggressive deals; risk stacking; reputational/legal exposure. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rule-bending / high-variance risk, high conflict temperature.
- **Friendships:** intensity cycles; sensitivity to slights; rupture–repair patterns; avoids direct talks; replays interactions; seeks certainty; boundary testing; impulsive comments or plans; conflict after crossings. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rule-bending / high-variance risk, high conflict temperature.
- **Hobbies:** frustration spikes; quits/pauses abruptly or pushes angrily; over-researches; delays starting; fear of doing it wrong; risky challenges; safety corners cut; extreme experimentation. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rule-bending / high-variance risk, high conflict temperature.
- **Romantic:** arguments ignite quickly; push–pull closeness; fast escalation; rumination and reassurance loops; ambiguous cues feel threatening; impulsive decisions/spending/flirting risks; commitment strain. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rule-bending / high-variance risk, high conflict temperature.
- **Overall lifestyle:** bursts and crashes; routines swing with mood and stress; narrower comfort routines; reduced novelty; mental load stays high; stimulation-heavy; difficulty with boring maintenance; volatility. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rule-bending / high-variance risk, high conflict temperature.
- **Health:** sleep disruption/tension; coping volatility (comfort behaviors or overcontrol); insomnia/tension; difficulty relaxing; stress symptoms persist; recovery neglected; risky coping; inconsistent sleep and routines. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rule-bending / high-variance risk, high conflict temperature.
- **Sports:** overreaches after setbacks; heat with coaches/partners; volatile load choices; conservative progression; inconsistent blocks from fear (injury/failure); trains through pain; overreaches; repeated injury or overtraining cycles. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rule-bending / high-variance risk, high conflict temperature.

**Strength edge (when regulated): risk awareness, speed and boldness, urgency and energy.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): slow closure / rumination, rule-bending / high-variance risk, high conflict temperature.**

## 6) **VR+WA+SS** — Volatile Reactivity + Worry-Driven Avoidance + Spotlight Seeking

**Signature:** alarm volatility with optics pressure

**Core loop:** uncertainty triggers worst-case thinking and hesitation → communication and self-presentation rise; optics management intensifies → conflict escalates and others experience unpredictability → this reinforces risk-averse and ruminative patterns.

- **Career:** tone spikes, defensiveness to feedback, performance variance across weeks; analysis paralysis; overchecking; delays hard calls and conflict; dominates airtime; pushes visibility; credit sensitivity; performative updates. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, optics pressure / validation dependence, high conflict temperature.
- **Business:** rapid pivots and escalation culture; urgency communicated with heat; slow launches; over-validation; missed windows from hesitation; optics-first instincts; narrative management; PR over ops risk. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, optics pressure / validation dependence, high conflict temperature.
- **Friendships:** intensity cycles; sensitivity to slights; rupture–repair patterns; avoids direct talks; replays interactions; seeks certainty; center-of-gravity behavior; sensitive to exclusion; attention competition. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, optics pressure / validation dependence, high conflict temperature.
- **Hobbies:** frustration spikes; quits/pauses abruptly or pushes angrily; over-researches; delays starting; fear of doing it wrong; chooses social/performative arenas; posts for validation. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, optics pressure / validation dependence, high conflict temperature.
- **Romantic:** arguments ignite quickly; push–pull closeness; fast escalation; rumination and reassurance loops; ambiguous cues feel threatening; needs admiration; conflict when ignored; attention jealousy. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, optics pressure / validation dependence, high conflict temperature.
- **Overall lifestyle:** bursts and crashes; routines swing with mood and stress; narrower comfort routines; reduced novelty; mental load stays high; busy social calendar; image-curation; overstimulation. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, optics pressure / validation dependence, high conflict temperature.
- **Health:** sleep disruption/tension; coping volatility (comfort behaviors or overcontrol); insomnia/tension; difficulty relaxing; stress symptoms persist; motivation depends on feedback; adherence drops when unseen. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, optics pressure / validation dependence, high conflict temperature.
- **Sports:** overreaches after setbacks; heat with coaches/partners; volatile load choices; conservative progression; inconsistent blocks from fear (injury/failure); thrives in competitions/classes; neglects boring base work. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, optics pressure / validation dependence, high conflict temperature.

**Strength edge (when regulated): risk awareness, rallying and communication, urgency and energy.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): slow closure / rumination, optics pressure / validation dependence, high conflict temperature.**

## 7) **VR+WA+UT** — Volatile Reactivity + Worry-Driven Avoidance + Unconventional Thinking

**Signature:** alarm volatility with unconventional framing

**Core loop:** uncertainty triggers worst-case thinking and hesitation → you generate big pivots/angles and may detach from practical constraints → conflict escalates and others experience unpredictability → this reinforces risk-averse and ruminative patterns.

- **Career:** tone spikes, defensiveness to feedback, performance variance across weeks; analysis paralysis; overchecking; delays hard calls and conflict; big conceptual leaps; skips steps; communication can be nonlinear. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, complexity / feasibility drift, high conflict temperature.
- **Business:** rapid pivots and escalation culture; urgency communicated with heat; slow launches; over-validation; missed windows from hesitation; visionary pivots; compelling narratives; execution instability risk. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, complexity / feasibility drift, high conflict temperature.
- **Friendships:** intensity cycles; sensitivity to slights; rupture–repair patterns; avoids direct talks; replays interactions; seeks certainty; abstract/intense idea-talk; unusual interpretations; misses practical cues. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, complexity / feasibility drift, high conflict temperature.
- **Hobbies:** frustration spikes; quits/pauses abruptly or pushes angrily; over-researches; delays starting; fear of doing it wrong; constant experimentation; low repetition/mastery. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, complexity / feasibility drift, high conflict temperature.
- **Romantic:** arguments ignite quickly; push–pull closeness; fast escalation; rumination and reassurance loops; ambiguous cues feel threatening; unpredictable routines; friction about practicality and follow-through. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, complexity / feasibility drift, high conflict temperature.
- **Overall lifestyle:** bursts and crashes; routines swing with mood and stress; narrower comfort routines; reduced novelty; mental load stays high; many projects; irregular structure; unfinished initiatives accumulate. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, complexity / feasibility drift, high conflict temperature.
- **Health:** sleep disruption/tension; coping volatility (comfort behaviors or overcontrol); insomnia/tension; difficulty relaxing; stress symptoms persist; "hack" chasing; protocol hopping; adherence suffers. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, complexity / feasibility drift, high conflict temperature.
- **Sports:** overreaches after setbacks; heat with coaches/partners; volatile load choices; conservative progression; inconsistent blocks from fear (injury/failure); inventive programming; ignores progressive overload/recovery; plateau/injury risk. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, complexity / feasibility drift, high conflict temperature.

**Strength edge (when regulated): originality and pattern finding, risk awareness, urgency and energy.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): slow closure / rumination, complexity / feasibility drift, high conflict temperature.**

## 8) **VR+WA+PC** — Volatile Reactivity + Worry-Driven Avoidance + Perfectionistic Control

**Signature:** heated micromanagement

**Core loop:** uncertainty triggers worst-case thinking and hesitation → standards rise, delegation drops, and you over-focus on correctness → conflict escalates and others experience unpredictability → this reinforces risk-averse and ruminative patterns.

- **Career:** tone spikes, defensiveness to feedback, performance variance across weeks; analysis paralysis; overchecking; delays hard calls and conflict; micromanages; slows delivery; difficulty delegating; critical feedback. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rigidity / bottlenecks, high conflict temperature.
- **Business:** rapid pivots and escalation culture; urgency communicated with heat; slow launches; over-validation; missed windows from hesitation; leader-as-qa gate; scaling bottlenecks; process creep. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rigidity / bottlenecks, high conflict temperature.
- **Friendships:** intensity cycles; sensitivity to slights; rupture–repair patterns; avoids direct talks; replays interactions; seeks certainty; judgmental corrections; rigid plans; low spontaneity. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rigidity / bottlenecks, high conflict temperature.
- **Hobbies:** frustration spikes; quits/pauses abruptly or pushes angrily; over-researches; delays starting; fear of doing it wrong; perfection blocks joy; procrastination via standards. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rigidity / bottlenecks, high conflict temperature.
- **Romantic:** arguments ignite quickly; push–pull closeness; fast escalation; rumination and reassurance loops; ambiguous cues feel threatening; controlling preferences; criticism of small things; autonomy conflict. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rigidity / bottlenecks, high conflict temperature.
- **Overall lifestyle:** bursts and crashes; routines swing with mood and stress; narrower comfort routines; reduced novelty; mental load stays high; brittle routines; stress when disrupted; constant checking. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rigidity / bottlenecks, high conflict temperature.
- **Health:** sleep disruption/tension; coping volatility (comfort behaviors or overcontrol); insomnia/tension; difficulty relaxing; stress symptoms persist; rigid diet/training rules; guilt cycles; recovery neglected. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rigidity / bottlenecks, high conflict temperature.
- **Sports:** overreaches after setbacks; heat with coaches/partners; volatile load choices; conservative progression; inconsistent blocks from fear (injury/failure); technique obsession; deload resistance; overuse injuries. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, rigidity / bottlenecks, high conflict temperature.

**Strength edge (when regulated): quality discipline, risk awareness, urgency and energy.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): slow closure / rumination, rigidity / bottlenecks, high conflict temperature.**

## 9) **VR+WA+AD** — Volatile Reactivity + Worry-Driven Avoidance + Approval Dependence

**Signature:** anxious appeasement with emotional heat

**Core loop:** uncertainty triggers worst-case thinking and hesitation → tone sharpens, patience drops, and reactions come fast → boundaries collapse and resentment/burnout build → this reinforces risk-averse and ruminative patterns.

- **Career:** tone spikes, defensiveness to feedback, performance variance across weeks; analysis paralysis; overchecking; delays hard calls and conflict; avoids disagreement; seeks alignment; takes on too much. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Business:** rapid pivots and escalation culture; urgency communicated with heat; slow launches; over-validation; missed windows from hesitation; strategy diluted to satisfy stakeholders; pricing/boundary issues. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Friendships:** intensity cycles; sensitivity to slights; rupture–repair patterns; avoids direct talks; replays interactions; seeks certainty; over-giving; difficulty expressing needs; resentment later. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Hobbies:** frustration spikes; quits/pauses abruptly or pushes angrily; over-researches; delays starting; fear of doing it wrong; chooses what fits in; less self-directed enjoyment. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Romantic:** arguments ignite quickly; push–pull closeness; fast escalation; rumination and reassurance loops; ambiguous cues feel threatening; reassurance needs; conflict avoidance; anxious closeness patterns. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Overall lifestyle:** bursts and crashes; routines swing with mood and stress; narrower comfort routines; reduced novelty; mental load stays high; packed obligations; low recovery; identity tied to being needed. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Health:** sleep disruption/tension; coping volatility (comfort behaviors or overcontrol); insomnia/tension; difficulty relaxing; stress symptoms persist; health goals sacrificed to social pressure; stress coping increases. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Sports:** overreaches after setbacks; heat with coaches/partners; volatile load choices; conservative progression; inconsistent blocks from fear (injury/failure); trains to impress; struggles to rest; overcommits and overtrains. Net effect: slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.

**Strength edge (when regulated): risk awareness, loyalty and service orientation, urgency and energy.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): slow closure / rumination, high conflict temperature, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.**

**Signature:** fortress mode with emotional heat

**Core loop:** stress increases vigilance and motive-reading → communication drops, you go quiet, and you handle things alone → conflict escalates and others experience unpredictability → this reinforces skeptical and distrustful patterns.

- **Career:** tone spikes, defensiveness to feedback, performance variance across weeks; low updates; quiet in meetings; others lack visibility into work; defensive interpretations of feedback; accusatory skepticism; paper trails. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, high conflict temperature.

**Signature:** withdrawn / resistant / reactive

## 12) **VR+IW+SI** — Volatile Reactivity + Interpersonal Withdrawal + Self-Importance

**Signature:** withdrawn / dominant / reactive

**Core loop:** emotional arousal spikes quickly under stress → communication drops, you go quiet, and you handle things alone → learning slows and relationships strain under arrogance or unilateralism → this reinforces emotionally intense and reactive patterns.

- **Career:** tone spikes, defensiveness to feedback, performance variance across weeks; low updates; quiet in meetings; others lack visibility into work; dominates airtime; dismisses advice; difficult to coach; credit sensitivity. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Business:** rapid pivots and escalation culture; urgency communicated with heat; stakeholders feel cut off; decisions happen privately; low transparency; founder/leader bottleneck; unilateral calls; talent disengagement. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Friendships:** intensity cycles; sensitivity to slights; rupture–repair patterns; slower replies; fewer initiations; disappears during busy periods; one-upmanship; low curiosity; difficulty apologizing. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Hobbies:** frustration spikes; quits/pauses abruptly or pushes angrily; prefers solo versions; avoids groups/communities when stressed; resists being a beginner; competitiveness disrupts learning. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Romantic:** arguments ignite quickly; push–pull closeness; fast escalation; shutdown during conflict; partner feels locked out; intimacy declines; power struggles; partner feels unseen or managed. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Overall lifestyle:** bursts and crashes; routines swing with mood and stress; social circle shrinks; solitude becomes default coping; status-oriented choices; impatience with constraints; reduced humility. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Health:** sleep disruption/tension; coping volatility (comfort behaviors or overcontrol); delays seeking help; under-communicates symptoms; low support use; ignores guidance; exception narratives; delayed preventive care. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.
- **Sports:** overreaches after setbacks; heat with coaches/partners; volatile load choices; trains alone; avoids coaching feedback; plateau risk from low input; ego loading; dismisses deloads; injury risk from overconfidence. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.

**Strength edge (when regulated): confidence and decisiveness, urgency and energy, independence and focus.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity, high conflict temperature.**

## 13) **VR+IW+BP** — Volatile Reactivity + Interpersonal Withdrawal + Boundary-Pushing

Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, rule-bending / high-variance risk, high conflict temperature.
- **Overall lifestyle:** bursts and crashes; routines swing with mood and stress; social circle shrinks; solitude becomes default coping; stimulation-heavy; difficulty with boring maintenance; volatility. **Derailer edge (when sustained): low trust / defensive interpretation, high conflict temperature, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.**

## 82) **IW+CG+PP** — Interpersonal Withdrawal + Cynical Guardedness + Passive Pushback

**Signature:** fortress mode

**Core loop:** stress increases vigilance and motive-reading → communication drops, you go quiet, and you handle things alone → hidden nonalignment creates friction and trust issues → this reinforces skeptical and distrustful patterns.

- **Career:** low updates; quiet in meetings; others lack visibility into work; defensive interpretations of feedback; accusatory skepticism; paper trails; "yes" in meetings, drift afterward; slow-roll; selective compliance. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, hidden nonalignment.
- **Business:** stakeholders feel cut off; decisions happen privately; low transparency; slow trust-building; hardball negotiations; information hoarding; stakeholders experience surprise nonalignment; forecasting and trust suffer. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, hidden nonalignment.
- **Friendships:** slower replies; fewer initiations; disappears during busy periods; tests loyalty; assumes slights; keeps score; avoids direct conflict; resentment leaks via sarcasm or cancellation. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, hidden nonalignment.
- **Hobbies:** prefers solo versions; avoids groups/communities when stressed; distrusts coaches/groups; assumes agendas; churns communities; ignores guidance; does it "my way" without renegotiating openly. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, hidden nonalignment.
- **Romantic:** shutdown during conflict; partner feels locked out; intimacy declines; jealousy/monitoring tendencies; conflicts about intent and trust; silent protest and procrastination; indirect retaliation; unspoken resentment. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, hidden nonalignment.
- **Overall lifestyle:** social circle shrinks; solitude becomes default coping; high vigilance; low spontaneity; control behaviors increase; resists imposed structure; oppositional routines; chronic friction. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, hidden nonalignment.
- **Health:** delays seeking help; under-communicates symptoms; low support use; mistrust of providers; second-guessing advice; nonadherence risk; inconsistent adherence if buy-in is low; rebellion breaks and resets. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, hidden nonalignment.
- **Sports:** trains alone; avoids coaching feedback; plateau risk from low input; argues with programming; interprets cues as criticism; coach conflict; cherry-picks training; avoids disliked sessions; low transparency about changes. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, hidden nonalignment.

**Strength edge (when regulated): due diligence and boundary detection, independence and focus, autonomy and independent judgment.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, hidden nonalignment.**

## 83) **IW+CG+SI** — Interpersonal Withdrawal + Cynical Guardedness + Self-Importance

**Signature:** fortress mode

**Core loop:** stress increases vigilance and motive-reading → communication drops, you go quiet, and you handle things alone → learning slows and relationships strain under arrogance or unilateralism → this reinforces skeptical and distrustful patterns.

- **Career:** low updates; quiet in meetings; others lack visibility into work; defensive interpretations of feedback; accusatory skepticism; paper trails; dominates airtime; dismisses advice; difficult to coach; credit sensitivity. - **Business:** stakeholders feel cut off; decisions happen privately; low transparency; slow trust-building; hardball negotiations; information hoarding; founder/leader bottleneck; unilateral calls; talent disengagement. - **Friendships:** slower replies; fewer initiations; disappears during busy periods; tests loyalty; assumes slights; keeps score; one-upmanship; low curiosity; difficulty apologizing. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity.
- **Hobbies:** prefers solo versions; avoids groups/communities when stressed; distrusts coaches/groups; assumes agendas; churns communities; resists being a beginner; competitiveness disrupts learning. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity.
- **Romantic:** shutdown during conflict; partner feels locked out; intimacy declines; jealousy/monitoring tendencies; conflicts about intent and trust; power struggles; partner feels unseen or managed. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity.
- **Overall lifestyle:** social circle shrinks; solitude becomes default coping; high vigilance; low spontaneity; control behaviors increase; status-oriented choices; impatience with constraints; reduced humility. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity.
- **Health:** delays seeking help; under-communicates symptoms; low support use; mistrust of providers; second-guessing advice; nonadherence risk; ignores guidance; exception narratives; delayed preventive care. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity.
- **Sports:** trains alone; avoids coaching feedback; plateau risk from low input; argues with programming; interprets cues as criticism; coach conflict; ego loading; dismisses deloads; injury risk from overconfidence. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity.

- **Hobbies:** prefers solo versions; avoids groups/communities when stressed; resists being a beginner; competitiveness disrupts learning; risky challenges; safety corners cut; extreme experimentation. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity, rule-bending / high-variance risk.

Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, dominance / low receptivity, rule-bending / high-variance risk.

**Derailer edge (when sustained): low transparency / disconnection, optics pressure / validation dependence, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.**

## 107) **IW+UT+PC** — Interpersonal Withdrawal + Unconventional Thinking + Perfectionistic Control

**Signature:** overengineering with withdrawal

**Core loop:** stress increases need for certainty through detail and control → communication drops, you go quiet, and you handle things alone → feasibility and consistency suffer; others can feel confused → this reinforces rigid and micromanaging patterns.

- **Career:** low updates; quiet in meetings; others lack visibility into work; big conceptual leaps; skips steps; communication can be nonlinear; micromanages; slows delivery; difficulty delegating; critical feedback. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift.
- **Business:** stakeholders feel cut off; decisions happen privately; low transparency; visionary pivots; compelling narratives; execution instability risk; leader-as-qa gate; scaling bottlenecks; process creep. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift.
- **Friendships:** slower replies; fewer initiations; disappears during busy periods; abstract/intense idea-talk; unusual interpretations; misses practical cues; judgmental corrections; rigid plans; low spontaneity. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift.
- **Hobbies:** prefers solo versions; avoids groups/communities when stressed; constant experimentation; low repetition/mastery; perfection blocks joy; procrastination via standards. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift.
- **Romantic:** shutdown during conflict; partner feels locked out; intimacy declines; unpredictable routines; friction about practicality and follow-through; controlling preferences; criticism of small things; autonomy conflict. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift.
- **Overall lifestyle:** social circle shrinks; solitude becomes default coping; many projects; irregular structure; unfinished initiatives accumulate; brittle routines; stress when disrupted; constant checking. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift.
- **Health:** delays seeking help; under-communicates symptoms; low support use; "hack" chasing; protocol hopping; adherence suffers; rigid diet/training rules; guilt cycles; recovery neglected. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift.
- **Sports:** trains alone; avoids coaching feedback; plateau risk from low input; inventive programming; ignores progressive overload/recovery; plateau/injury risk; technique obsession; deload resistance; overuse injuries. Net effect: low transparency / disconnection, rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift.

## 110) **CG+PP+SI** — Cynical Guardedness + Passive Pushback + Self-Importance

**Signature:** covert distrust

**Core loop:** stress increases vigilance and motive-reading → you agree outwardly but resist through delay, reinterpretation, or nonfollow-through → learning slows and relationships strain under arrogance or unilateralism → this reinforces skeptical and distrustful patterns.

- **Career:** defensive interpretations of feedback; accusatory skepticism; paper trails; "yes" in meetings, drift afterward; slow-roll; selective compliance; dominates airtime; dismisses advice; difficult to coach; credit sensitivity. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity.
- **Business:** slow trust-building; hardball negotiations; information hoarding; stakeholders experience surprise nonalignment; forecasting and trust suffer; founder/leader bottleneck; unilateral calls; talent disengagement. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity.
- **Friendships:** tests loyalty; assumes slights; keeps score; avoids direct conflict; resentment leaks via sarcasm or cancellation; one-upmanship; low curiosity; difficulty apologizing. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity.
- **Hobbies:** distrusts coaches/groups; assumes agendas; churns communities; ignores guidance; does it "my way" without renegotiating openly; resists being a beginner; competitiveness disrupts learning. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity.
- **Romantic:** jealousy/monitoring tendencies; conflicts about intent and trust; silent protest and procrastination; indirect retaliation; unspoken resentment; power struggles; partner feels unseen or managed. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity.
- **Overall lifestyle:** high vigilance; low spontaneity; control behaviors increase; resists imposed structure; oppositional routines; chronic friction; status-oriented choices; impatience with constraints; reduced humility. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity.
- **Health:** mistrust of providers; second-guessing advice; nonadherence risk; inconsistent adherence if buy-in is low; rebellion breaks and resets; ignores guidance; exception narratives; delayed preventive care. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity.
- **Sports:** argues with programming; interprets cues as criticism; coach conflict; cherry-picks training; avoids disliked sessions; low transparency about changes; ego loading; dismisses deloads; injury risk from overconfidence. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity.

**Strength edge (when regulated): due diligence and boundary detection, confidence and decisiveness, autonomy and independent judgment.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): low trust / defensive interpretation, hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity.**

Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, dominance / low receptivity, complexity / feasibility drift.

Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, rigidity / bottlenecks, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Friendships:** tests loyalty; assumes slights; keeps score; judgmental corrections; rigid plans; low spontaneity; over-giving; difficulty expressing needs; resentment later. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, rigidity / bottlenecks, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Hobbies:** distrusts coaches/groups; assumes agendas; churns communities; perfection blocks joy; procrastination via standards; chooses what fits in; less self-directed enjoyment. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, rigidity / bottlenecks, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Romantic:** jealousy/monitoring tendencies; conflicts about intent and trust; controlling preferences; criticism of small things; autonomy conflict; reassurance needs; conflict avoidance; anxious closeness patterns. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, rigidity / bottlenecks, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Overall lifestyle:** high vigilance; low spontaneity; control behaviors increase; brittle routines; stress when disrupted; constant checking; packed obligations; low recovery; identity tied to being needed. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, rigidity / bottlenecks, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Health:** mistrust of providers; second-guessing advice; nonadherence risk; rigid diet/training rules; guilt cycles; recovery neglected; health goals sacrificed to social pressure; stress coping increases. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, rigidity / bottlenecks, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Sports:** argues with programming; interprets cues as criticism; coach conflict; technique obsession; deload resistance; overuse injuries; trains to impress; struggles to rest; overcommits and overtrains. Net effect: low trust / defensive interpretation, rigidity / bottlenecks, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.

**Strength edge (when regulated): quality discipline, due diligence and boundary detection, loyalty and service orientation.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): low trust / defensive interpretation, rigidity / bottlenecks, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.**

## 131) **PP+SI+BP** — Passive Pushback + Self-Importance + Boundary-Pushing

**Signature:** rule-bending entitlement

**Core loop:** stress increases certainty, status sensitivity, and control needs → you agree outwardly but resist through delay, reinterpretation, or nonfollow-through → ethics/compliance and safety risks rise; trust can be damaged → this reinforces dominant and entitled patterns.

- **Career:** "yes" in meetings, drift afterward; slow-roll; selective compliance; dominates airtime; dismisses advice; difficult to coach; credit sensitivity; cuts corners; compliance friction; "ask forgiveness" pattern. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity, rule-bending / high-variance risk.
- **Business:** stakeholders experience surprise nonalignment; forecasting and trust suffer; founder/leader bottleneck; unilateral calls; talent disengagement; aggressive deals; risk stacking; reputational/legal exposure. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity, rule-bending / high-variance risk.
- **Friendships:** avoids direct conflict; resentment leaks via sarcasm or cancellation; one-upmanship; low curiosity; difficulty apologizing; boundary testing; impulsive comments or plans; conflict after crossings. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity, rule-bending / high-variance risk.
- **Hobbies:** ignores guidance; does it "my way" without renegotiating openly; resists being a beginner; competitiveness disrupts learning; risky challenges; safety corners cut; extreme experimentation. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity, rule-bending / high-variance risk.
- **Romantic:** silent protest and procrastination; indirect retaliation; unspoken resentment; power struggles; partner feels unseen or managed; impulsive decisions/spending/flirting risks; commitment strain. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity, rule-bending / high-variance risk.
- **Overall lifestyle:** resists imposed structure; oppositional routines; chronic friction; status-oriented choices; impatience with constraints; reduced humility; stimulation-heavy; difficulty with boring maintenance; volatility. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity, rule-bending / high-variance risk.
- **Health:** inconsistent adherence if buy-in is low; rebellion breaks and resets; ignores guidance; exception narratives; delayed preventive care; recovery neglected; risky coping; inconsistent sleep and routines. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity, rule-bending / high-variance risk.
- **Sports:** cherry-picks training; avoids disliked sessions; low transparency about changes; ego loading; dismisses deloads; injury risk from overconfidence; trains through pain; overreaches; repeated injury or overtraining cycles. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity, rule-bending / high-variance risk.

**Derailer edge (when sustained): hidden nonalignment, dominance / low receptivity, rule-bending / high-variance risk.**

- **Sports:** cherry-picks training; avoids disliked sessions; low transparency about changes; thrives in competitions/classes; neglects boring base work; technique obsession; deload resistance; overuse injuries. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, rigidity / bottlenecks, optics pressure / validation dependence.

**Strength edge (when regulated): quality discipline, rallying and communication, autonomy and independent judgment.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): hidden nonalignment, rigidity / bottlenecks, optics pressure / validation dependence.**

## 142) **PP+SS+AD** — Passive Pushback + Spotlight Seeking + Approval Dependence

**Signature:** validation hunger

**Core loop:** stress increases fear of disappointing others and need for reassurance → you agree outwardly but resist through delay, reinterpretation, or nonfollow-through → theatrics, credit conflicts, and dependence on attention increase → this reinforces reassurance-seeking and people-pleasing patterns.

- **Career:** "yes" in meetings, drift afterward; slow-roll; selective compliance; dominates airtime; pushes visibility; credit sensitivity; performative updates; avoids disagreement; seeks alignment; takes on too much. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, optics pressure / validation dependence, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Business:** stakeholders experience surprise nonalignment; forecasting and trust suffer; optics-first instincts; narrative management; PR over ops risk; strategy diluted to satisfy stakeholders; pricing/boundary issues. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, optics pressure / validation dependence, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Friendships:** avoids direct conflict; resentment leaks via sarcasm or cancellation; center-of-gravity behavior; sensitive to exclusion; attention competition; over-giving; difficulty expressing needs; resentment later. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, optics pressure / validation dependence, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Hobbies:** ignores guidance; does it "my way" without renegotiating openly; chooses social/performative arenas; posts for validation; chooses what fits in; less self-directed enjoyment. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, optics pressure / validation dependence, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Romantic:** silent protest and procrastination; indirect retaliation; unspoken resentment; needs admiration; conflict when ignored; attention jealousy; reassurance needs; conflict avoidance; anxious closeness patterns. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, optics pressure / validation dependence, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Overall lifestyle:** resists imposed structure; oppositional routines; chronic friction; busy social calendar; image-curation; overstimulation; packed obligations; low recovery; identity tied to being needed. Net effect: hidden nonalignment, optics pressure / validation dependence, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Health:** inconsistent adherence if buy-in is low; rebellion breaks and resets; motivation depends on feedback; adherence drops when unseen; health goals sacrificed to social pressure; stress coping increases. - **Sports:** thrives in competitions/classes; neglects boring base work; technique obsession; deload resistance; overuse injuries; trains to impress; struggles to rest; overcommits and overtrains. Net effect: rigidity / bottlenecks, optics pressure / validation dependence, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.

**Strength edge (when regulated): quality discipline, loyalty and service orientation, rallying and communication.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): rigidity / bottlenecks, optics pressure / validation dependence, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.**

## 165) **UT+PC+AD** — Unconventional Thinking + Perfectionistic Control + Approval Dependence

**Signature:** overengineering

**Core loop:** stress increases fear of disappointing others and need for reassurance → standards rise, delegation drops, and you over-focus on correctness → feasibility and consistency suffer; others can feel confused → this reinforces reassurance-seeking and people-pleasing patterns.

- **Career:** big conceptual leaps; skips steps; communication can be nonlinear; micromanages; slows delivery; difficulty delegating; critical feedback; avoids disagreement; seeks alignment; takes on too much. Net effect: rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Business:** visionary pivots; compelling narratives; execution instability risk; leader-as-qa gate; scaling bottlenecks; process creep; strategy diluted to satisfy stakeholders; pricing/boundary issues. Net effect: rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Friendships:** abstract/intense idea-talk; unusual interpretations; misses practical cues; judgmental corrections; rigid plans; low spontaneity; over-giving; difficulty expressing needs; resentment later. Net effect: rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Hobbies:** constant experimentation; low repetition/mastery; perfection blocks joy; procrastination via standards; chooses what fits in; less self-directed enjoyment. Net effect: rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Romantic:** unpredictable routines; friction about practicality and follow-through; controlling preferences; criticism of small things; autonomy conflict; reassurance needs; conflict avoidance; anxious closeness patterns. Net effect: rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Overall lifestyle:** many projects; irregular structure; unfinished initiatives accumulate; brittle routines; stress when disrupted; constant checking; packed obligations; low recovery; identity tied to being needed. Net effect: rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Health:** "hack" chasing; protocol hopping; adherence suffers; rigid diet/training rules; guilt cycles; recovery neglected; health goals sacrificed to social pressure; stress coping increases. Net effect: rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.
- **Sports:** inventive programming; ignores progressive overload/recovery; plateau/injury risk; technique obsession; deload resistance; overuse injuries; trains to impress; struggles to rest; overcommits and overtrains. Net effect: rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.

**Strength edge (when regulated): originality and pattern finding, quality discipline, loyalty and service orientation.**  
**Derailer edge (when sustained): rigidity / bottlenecks, complexity / feasibility drift, people-pleasing / boundary erosion.**
